## Diagram 3

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant Caller
    participant DealerCSVMocker
    Caller->>DealerCSVMocker: instantiate()
    Caller->>DealerCSVMocker: mock_full_event()
    DealerCSVMocker->>DealerCSVMocker: mock_data_to_string()
    DealerCSVMocker->>DealerCSVMocker: gen_mock_data()
    DealerCSVMocker->>DealerCSVMocker: generate_dealer_name()
    DealerCSVMocker->>DealerCSVMocker: generate_location_name_with_dealer()
    DealerCSVMocker->>DealerCSVMocker: dataframe_to_string()
    DealerCSVMocker-->>Caller: return event dict
```

## Diagram 4

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
    [*] --> Idle
    Idle --> Generating : mock_full_event called
    Generating --> BuildingDict : gen_mock_data()
    BuildingDict --> Transforming : map dealer & location names
    Transforming --> Converting : dict_of_lists_to_list_of_dicts
    Converting --> Returning : return dummy_data
    Returning --> Idle
```
